          <td id="LC398" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">   We use void pointers because of its reusability. Void pointers can store the object of any type, and</td>
        </tr>

          <td id="L399" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="399"></td>
